The guard sighs. "You're right. I was sitting at home, on the internet like usual, when I saw an advertisement that promised me power and satisfaction with my life. I thought that I might as well, since I had nothing better to do. But then they threatened to kill me when I said I wanted to leave. You know what though? Here." The man throws you his robes. "I just want to go home. The buttons you have to press are the one with the candles lit at the top and bottom, and the one with the star, the triangle, the circle, the square and the cross. Good luck." The man walks off in the direction from which you came with nothing but his pistol and his book. The top 5 pentagrams have lit flames on various points, while the bottom 5 have various symbols on each point. "My name is Hannibal, I'm a scholar, and I've been studying the Wizard Agrippa for most of my career. And that [[journal|What is this journal?]] contains almost all of that work. I can't go without it, and [[those people|Who are the attackers?]] stole it from me!" He seems to be on the verge of tears. Do you want to [[help him]]?\n\n[img[protagonism]] [img[sad_agrippa]]
The guard sighs. "You know what? Whatever." He takes off his robes. "Put these on. Do whatever you'd like. I just don't wanna be here anymore." The guard walks off with only his pistol tucked into his waistband and his book in his hand. You put on the robes and [[walk inside|First steps: Talking edition]].
The last story is a high-seas tale of adventure, with the tall cowboy sailing through the seas in search of an evil magician. Just as you close the book, satisfied, you hear a shuffling. A smack, and then darkness. You wake up what must be hours later with nothing but your underwear, and with the cultists nowhere to be found. Well then. Better go get some new gear. Your adventure is over.

There's only one story left though! [[Keep reading?|Keep reading 4]] Or do you [[stop reading|Stop reading]], even though you're so close?\n\n[img[book]]
The next tale is of a thundering metal steed that terrorizes the population of a frontier town. You've been reading for a while now, but it's really gripping. [[Keep reading?|Keep reading 3]] Or [[stop?|Stop reading]]\n\n[img[book]]
You are now at what qualifies as the top of the tower, and by "top", you mean the second floor, that being the last above-ground floor still standing. There's not much up here, except some [[scraps of paper|Papes on the tower]] and a [[pentagram|Examining the pentagram]]. Wanna [[head back down|First step into the ruins]]?

"I'm not entirely sure who the people who stole [[it|What is this journal?]] were, as they hit me over the back of my shell, although [[I|Who is this scholar?]] have a pretty good idea. There's a cult that sprung up around Agrippa, with the intention of somehow further developing his spectrification spell. I don't know much more than that." The man is on the verge of tears. You call a hello to the old man, and tell him you're here to get the book back. "Ah... I-I see. I knew you would come eventually. I'm sorry for all the trouble I caused." Upon asking him why he started this cult, he explains that he did it to try and reanimate his wife. That's kind of a cliche, isn't it? "You can have the book. There's not much more I can do anyway. Maybe it's time to move on." You take the book and [[move along|The End - Part 1]].
The button makes a satisfying clunk when you press it. What button do you press on the bottom?\n[[Star, triangle, circle, square, crab|Button Success2]]\n[[Crab, boat, hat, triangle, flame|Button Failure2]]\n[[Star, star, star, star, star|Button Failure2]]\n[[Ocean, crab, ocean, crab, star|Button Failure2]]\n[[Triangle, circle, star, flame, crab|Button Failure2]]\n\n[img[buttons]]
You walk up to the old man and cut him down. He doesn't even put up a fight. Ouch. You grab the book before too much blood gets on it and [[head back for the town|The End - Part 1]].
You are now at what qualifies as the top of the tower, and by "top", you mean the second floor, that being the last above-ground floor still standing. There's not much up here, except some [[scraps of paper|Papes on the tower - talking]] and a [[pentagram|Examining the pentagram - talking ]]. It's a standard pentagram, with candles on all 5 points, but only the one at the top point and the bottom two are lit. What could this mean? You should [[keep looking around|Sub-level 1]].\n\n[img[candle pentagram]]
The one on the left falls just as she's lining up her shot. Now that those folks are out of the way, you can [[head into the tower|First steps - killing edition]] if you'd like. You pick up a piece of parchment off the ground. There is some writing in the common tongue on it, in what appears to be Carcinus handwriting. It says: "At last, I've completed my work! I have reanimated the dead. Maybe now I shan't be so lonely. Unfortunately, I appear to have reanimated some who would rather have not been reanimated. I think I may nee-". The rest of the parchment is burned to a crisp. You put it back on the ground and [[continue looking around|Ascend the tower]].\n\n[img[parchment]]
You walk down into the sublevel. The two guards barely notice your presence. Do you want to examine the [[pentagram on the floor|Talkingpentagram]], the [[door on the wall]] or the [[parchment in the middle|Talkingparchment]]? You can also [[head back up|First steps: Talking edition]].
Harry Thoemmes
The door grinds open, shuddering as it goes. Looks like there's [[one more floor below you|Sub-level 2]].\n\n[img[protagonism]]
You enter the burnt, quiet tower. There's maybe a [[floor or two above you|Ascend the tower - killing edition]], but theres apparently at least one [[sub-level|Descend the tower - killing edition]] below you, based on the stairs.\n\n[img[protagonism]]
Between the time you killed the guy charging you, the lady with the ray gun got a bead on you. Two blasts to your chest does you in right quick. Your adventure is over.
